\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8cc_source_l00038}00038 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8cc_source_l00039}00039 \textcolor{comment}{/* All symbols defined below should begin with yy or YY, to avoid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8cc_source_l00040}00040 \textcolor{comment}{   infringing on user name space.  This should be done even for local}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8cc_source_l00041}00041 \textcolor{comment}{   variables, as they might otherwise be expanded by user macros.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8cc_source_l00042}00042 \textcolor{comment}{   There are some unavoidable exceptions within include files to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8cc_source_l00043}00043 \textcolor{comment}{   define necessary library symbols; they are noted "{}INFRINGES ON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8cc_source_l00044}00044 \textcolor{comment}{   USER NAME SPACE"{} below.  */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8cc_source_l01389}01389 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# ifndef yytnamerr}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8cc_source_l01390}01390 \textcolor{comment}{/* Copy to YYRES the contents of YYSTR after stripping away unnecessary}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8cc_source_l01391}01391 \textcolor{comment}{   quotes and backslashes, so that it's suitable for yyerror.  The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8cc_source_l01392}01392 \textcolor{comment}{   heuristic is that double-\/quoting is unnecessary unless the string}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8cc_source_l01393}01393 \textcolor{comment}{   contains an apostrophe, a comma, or backslash (other than}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8cc_source_l01394}01394 \textcolor{comment}{   backslash-\/backslash).  YYSTR is taken from yytname.  If YYRES is}}
